<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has articles on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/home_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:home (disambiguation)">home</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/home_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:home (disambiguation)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a title="ham">hƒÅm</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, hamlet, manor, estate, home, class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">home, village</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">h≈çm</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/(h)…ô äm/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">home</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/homes#English" title="homes">homes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heading</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>A <a href="/wiki/dwelling" title="dwelling">dwelling</a>.</i>
<ol><li>One‚Äôs own <a href="/wiki/dwell" title="dwell">dwelling</a> place; the <a href="/wiki/house" title="house">house</a> or structure in which one <a href="/wiki/live" title="live">lives</a>; especially the house in which one lives with his <a href="/wiki/family" title="family">family</a>; the habitual <a href="/wiki/abode" title="abode">abode</a> of one‚Äôs family; also, one‚Äôs <a href="/wiki/birthplace" title="birthplace">birthplace</a>.
<ul><li><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary">c.</a></i> <b>1526</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Tyndale" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Tyndale">William Tyndale</a>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Bible_(Tyndale)/John" class="extiw" title="s:Bible (Tyndale)/John">Bible: John</a> 22:10:
<dl><dd>And the disciples wet awaye agayne vnto their awne <b>home</b>.</dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd>Thither for ease and soft repose we come: / <b>Home</b> is the sacred refuge of our life; / Secured from all approaches, but a wife.</dd></dl></li>

<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1892</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Besant" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Besant">Walter Besant</a>,  ‚ÄúPrologue: Who is Edmund Gray?‚Äù, in  <cite>The Ivory Gate: A Novel</cite>, New York, N.Y.&#58; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper_(publisher)" class="extiw" title="w:Harper (publisher)">Harper &amp; Brothers</a>,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="Franklin Square">‚Ä¶</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/16832619">16832619</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://archive.org/stream/ivorygatenovel00besa#page/16/mode/1up/">page 16</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Athelstan Arundel walked <b>home</b> all the way, foaming and raging. <li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> June 29,  ‚Äú<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.economist.com/news/asia/21580209-natural-disaster-aggravated-poor-response-high-and-wet">High and wet</a>‚Äù, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Economist" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Economist">The Economist</a></cite>, volume 407, number 8842, page 28:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>

<li>The place where a person was <a href="/wiki/raise" title="raise">raised</a>; <a href="/wiki/childhood" title="childhood">childhood</a> or <a href="/wiki/parental" title="parental">parental</a> home; home of one‚Äôs parents or <a href="/wiki/guardian" title="guardian">guardian</a>.

<dl><dd>The rights listed in the UNCRC cover all areas of children's lives such as their right to have a <b>home</b> and their right to be educated.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>

<li>One‚Äôs <a href="/wiki/native" title="native">native</a> land; the place or <a href="/wiki/country" title="country">country</a> in which one dwells; the place where one‚Äôs ancestors dwell or dwelt.

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">home</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3&#124;s&#124;pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/homes#English" title="homes">homes</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/homing#English" title="homing">homing</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past&#124;and&#124;past&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/homed#English" title="homed">homed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">always&#32;&#32;with "in on"<span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/seek" title="seek">seek</a> or aim for something.
<dl><dd><i>The missile was able to <b>home</b> in on the target.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2008</b> July, Ewen Callaway, <i>New Scientist</i>:
<dl><dd>Much like a heat-seeking missile, a new kind of particle <b>homes in</b> on the blood vessels that nourish aggressive cancers, before unleashing a cell-destroying drug.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">home</strong> (<i>not <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of or pertaining to one‚Äôs <a href="/wiki/dwelling" title="dwelling">dwelling</a> or <a href="/wiki/country" title="country">country</a>; <a href="/wiki/domestic" title="domestic">domestic</a>; not <a href="/wiki/foreign" title="foreign">foreign</a>; as home manufactures; home comforts.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/close" title="close">Close</a>; <a href="/wiki/personal" title="personal">personal</a>; <a href="/wiki/pointed" title="pointed">pointed</a>.
<dl><dd><i>a <a href="/wiki/home_thrust" title="home thrust">home thrust</a></i></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Adverb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">home</strong> (<i>not <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>to <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/home#English" title="home">home</a></span>
<ol><li>to one's place of <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/residence#English" title="residence">residence</a></span> or one's customary or official location
<dl><dd><i><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/go_home#English" title="go home">go home</a></span></i>, <i>come home</i>, <i>carry home</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1863</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nathaniel_Hawthorne" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nathaniel Hawthorne">Nathaniel Hawthorne</a>, <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/cache/epub/8090/pg8090.txt">Our Old Home: A Series of English Sketches</a></i>,
<dl><dd>He made no complaint of his ill-fortune, but only repeated in a quiet voice, with a pathos of which he was himself evidently unconscious, "I want to get <b>home</b> to Ninety-second Street, Philadelphia."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>to one's place of birth</li>
<li>to the place where it <a href="/wiki/belong" title="belong">belongs</a>; to the end of a course; to the full length
<dl><dd><i>to drive a nail <b>home</b></i>; <i>to ram a cartridge <b>home</b></i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>c.1603</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a> <i>The Tragedy of Othello, The Moor of Venice</i>, Act 5, Scene 1,
<dl><dd>Wear thy good rapier bare, and put it <b>home</b>: <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>‚Ä¶<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1988</b>, Roald Dahl, <i>Matilda</i>
<dl><dd>Eventually she managed to slide the lid of the pencil-box right <b>home</b> and the newt was hers. Then, on second thoughts, she opened the lid just the tiniest fraction so that the creature could breathe.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Internet" title="Internet">Internet</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to the <a href="/wiki/home_page" title="home page">home page</a>
<dl><dd><i>Click here to go <b>home</b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol></li>
<li>in one's place of <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/residence#English" title="residence">residence</a></span> or one's customary or official location; <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/at_home#English" title="at home">at home</a></span>
<dl><dd><i>Everyone's gone to watch the game; there's nobody <b>home</b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>To a full and intimate degree; to the heart of the matter; <a href="/wiki/fully" title="fully">fully</a>, <a href="/wiki/directly" title="directly">directly</a>.
<ul><li><b>1625</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Bacon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Francis Bacon">Francis Bacon</a>, dedication to the Duke of Buckingham, in <i>Essays Civil and Moral</i>,
<dl><dd>I do now publish my Essays; which of all my other works have been most current&#160;: for that, as it seems, they come <b>home</b> to men's business and bosoms.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1718</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_South" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert South">Robert South</a>, <i>Twelve Sermons Preached at Several Times, And upon ·∫õeveral Occasions</i>,
<dl><dd>How <b>home</b> the charge reaches us, has been made out by ·∫õhewing with what high impudence ·∫õome among·∫õt us defend sin, ...</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1748</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Richardson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuel Richardson">Samuel Richardson</a>, <i>Clarissa</i>, Letter 67:
<dl><dd>Her treatment of you, you say, does no credit either to her education or fine sense. Very <b>home</b> put, truly!</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/soccer" title="soccer">soccer</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> into the <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/goal#English" title="goal">goal</a></span>
<ul><li><b>2004</b>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/football/eng_prem/3496755.stm">Tottenham 4-4 Leicester</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BBC_Sport" class="extiw" title="w:BBC Sport">BBC Sport</a>: February,
<dl><dd>Walker was penalised for a picking up a Gerry Taggart backpass and from the resulting free-kick, Keane fired <b>home</b> after Johnnie Jackson's initial effort was blocked.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/nautical" title="nautical">nautical</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> into the right, proper or <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/stowed#English" title="stowed">stowed</a></span> position
<dl><dd><i>sails sheeted <b>home</b></i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/home#English" title="home">Home</a></i> is often used in the formation of compound words, many of which need no special definition; as, home-brewed, home-built, home-grown, etc.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Asturian">Asturian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Asturian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Catalan">Catalan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Catalan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Catalan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Catalan">Old Catalan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-oca"><a href="/wiki/home#Old_Catalan" title="home">home</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-oca"><a href="/wiki/hom#Old_Catalan" title="hom">hom</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro"><a href="/wiki/omne#Old_Occitan" title="omne">omne</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro"><a href="/wiki/ome#Old_Occitan" title="ome">ome</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/homo#Latin" title="homo">hom≈ç</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/hominem#Latin" title="hominem">hominem</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">human being</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Old Latin">Old Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="itc-ola"><a href="/wiki/hemo#Old_Latin" title="hemo">hem≈ç</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Italic language">Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="itc-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Italic/hem%C5%8D" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Italic/hem≈ç">*hem≈ç</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/%C7%B5%CA%B0m%E1%B9%93" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/«µ ∞m·πì">*«µ ∞m·πì</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">earthling</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Balearic_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Balearic dialect">Balearic</a><span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Catalan" class="extiw" title="w:Central Catalan">Central</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Catalan_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Catalan pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/Àà…î.m…ô/</span></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Finnish">Finnish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Finnish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><span id="fi-index" class="langindex">(<a href="/wiki/Index:Finnish/h/o" title="Index:Finnish/h/o">index ho</a>)</span>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Finnic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Finnic language">Proto-Finnic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fiu-fin-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Finnic/homeh" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Finnic/homeh">*homeh</a></i>, from earlier <i>*≈°ome≈°</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/swammaz" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/swammaz">*swammaz</a></i> or earlier Pre-Germanic. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karelian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Karelian language">Karelian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="krl"><a href="/w/index.php?title=homeh&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="homeh (page does not exist)">homeh</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Veps_language" class="extiw" title="w:Veps language">Veps</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="vep"><a href="/w/index.php?title=homeh&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="homeh (page does not exist)">homeh</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Finnish_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Finnish pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ÀàhomeÀ£/</span>, <span class="IPA">[ÀàhoÃûmeÃû( î)]</span></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Galician">Galician</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Galician">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg/220px-Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="299" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg/330px-Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg/440px-Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2258" data-file-height="3070" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Da_Vinci_Vitruve_Luc_Viatour.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><i>Home</i> ("man")</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From Old Galician and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galician-Portuguese" class="extiw" title="w:Galician-Portuguese">Old Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-opt"><a href="/wiki/ome#Old_Portuguese" title="ome">ome</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="roa-opt"><a href="/wiki/om%E1%BA%BDe#Old_Portuguese" title="om·∫Ωe">om·∫Ωe</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/homo#Latin" title="homo">hom≈ç</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/hominem#Latin" title="hominem">hominem</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_4">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galician_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Galician phonology">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/Àà…î.m…™/</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"/><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: bottom; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio</td><td class="audiofile"><div class="mediaContainer" style="width:175px"><audio id="mwe_player_2" controls="" preload="none" style="width:175px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="0.66176870748299" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="gl-home.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/9c/Gl-home.ogg" type="audio/ogg; codecs=&quot;vorbis&quot;" data-title="Original Ogg file (138 kbps)" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="138078" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/9/9c/Gl-home.ogg/Gl-home.ogg.mp3" type="audio/mpeg" data-title="MP3" data-shorttitle="MP3" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" data-height="0" /></audio></div></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:gl-home.ogg" title="File:gl-home.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gl">home</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-gl p-form-of" lang="gl"><a href="/wiki/homes#Galician" title="homes">homes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/human" title="human">human</a>; <a href="/wiki/person" title="person">person</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gl">Unha sebe tres anos dura; un can tres sebes; unha mula tres cans; un <b>home</b> tres mulas.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ‚Äï <span class="e-translation">A hedge last for three years, a can for three hedges, a mule for three dogs, a person for three mules</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/mankind" title="mankind">mankind</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gl">O <b>home</b> chegou √° Lua en 1969.</i> ‚Äï <span class="e-translation"><b>Mankind</b> arrived to the Moon in 1969.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/man" title="man">man</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">adult male</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gl"><b>Home</b> casado muller √©.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ‚Äï <span class="e-translation">Married <b>man</b> woman is.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/male" title="male">male</a> human
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gl"><b>Home</b> pequeno fol de veleno.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ‚Äï <span class="e-translation">Small <b>man</b>, skin [bag] of venon.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/husband" title="husband">husband</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gl">√âste √© o meu <b>home</b>, Xaqu√≠n.</i> ‚Äï <span class="e-translation">This is my <b>husband</b>, Joachim.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><b>Home</b> is a <a href="/wiki/false_friend" title="false friend">false friend</a>, and does not mean <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/home#English" title="home">home</a></i>. <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Interjection">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gl">home</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/man" title="man">man</a>! <span class="use-with-mention">Expresses surprise, or mild annoyance</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="gl">-Es o campi√≥n do mundo? Contento? -<b>Home</b>!...</i> ‚Äï <span class="e-translation">-You're the champion of the world? Are you happy? -<b>Man</b>!... [Of course I'm happy, what kind of question is this?]</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_10">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/hominem#Latin" title="hominem">hominem</a></i>, accusative singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/homo#Latin" title="homo">hom≈ç</a></i>, with the loss of the <i>-in-</i> syllable. The nominative form <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/hom#Old_French" title="hom">hom</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/om#Old_French" title="om">om</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/on#Old_French" title="on">on</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/hon#Old_French" title="hon">hon</a></i> derives from the Latin nominative <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/homo#Latin" title="homo">hom≈ç</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_5">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Old French phonology">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/Àào.m…ô/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fro">home</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>oblique plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/homes#Old_French" title="homes">homes</a></b>, <i>nominative singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/hom#Old_French" title="hom">hom</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><strong class="selflink">home</strong></b>)
</p><p><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">oblique case</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/man" title="man">man</a> (male adult human being)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/man" title="man">man</a> (mankind; <i>Homo sapiens</i>)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>circa 1120</b>,  Philippe de Taon,  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://bestiary.ca/etexts/wright1841/bestiary%20of%20philippe%20de%20thaon%20-%20wright.pdf">Bestiaire</a></cite>, line 476:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="fro"><span class="Latn" lang="fro">O <b>HOM</b> de sancte vie, entent que signefie</span></span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">O MAN of sacred life, listen to what this means</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Old_Occitan">Old Occitan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Old Occitan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_14">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=home&amp;action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
